*Club domestic league appearances and goals, correct as of 14:38, 19 May 2025 (UTC)<br> National team caps and goals, correct as of 13:44, 22 November 2024 (UTC)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Florian Richard Wirtz</b> (born 3 May 2003) is a German professional <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> club <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany national team</a>.
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Early_life">Early life</h2></div>
<p>Wirtz was born in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brauweiler" title="Brauweiler">Brauweiler</a> district of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pulheim" title="Pulheim">Pulheim</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Rhine-Westphalia" title="North Rhine-Westphalia">North Rhine-Westphalia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WF_3-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-WF-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Club_career">Club career</h2></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Early_career">Early career</h3></div>
<p>Regarded as a big talent in German football, Wirtz joined the youth team of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1._FC_K%C3%B6ln" title="1. FC Kln">1. FC Kln</a> in 2010, where he remained until he was signed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> in January 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-Wonderkid_4-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-Wonderkid-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> His transfer to Leverkusen was controversial, as Kln felt that Leverkusen violated a gentleman's agreement between the two clubs in signing Wirtz.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2020:_Professional_debut">2020: Professional debut</h4></div>
<p>After impressing for the under-17 team, Wirtz made his senior professional debut for Leverkusen in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> on 18 May 2020, starting in an away match against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> In doing so, he overtook <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kai_Havertz" title="Kai Havertz">Kai Havertz</a> as Leverkusen's youngest player in the league, at the age of 17 years and 15 days.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 6 June, Wirtz scored his first goal for Leverkusen in the 89th minute of their 42 home loss against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>, making Wirtz the youngest goalscorer in Bundesliga history at the age of 17 years and 34 days.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> This record would later be surpassed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Youssoufa_Moukoko" title="Youssoufa Moukoko">Youssoufa Moukoko</a> less than a year later, aged 16 years and 28 days.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 22 October, he scored his first goal in European competitions in a 62 win over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a> during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Europa_League" title="202021 UEFA Europa League">202021 Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="202023:_Contract_extension_and_long-term_injury"><span id="2020.E2.80.9323:_Contract_extension_and_long-term_injury"></span>202023: Contract extension and long-term injury</h4></div>
<p>Wirtz signed a contract extension with the club on 23 December 2020, extending his deal until 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 19 January 2021, he scored the winner in the 80th minute of Leverkusen's 21 home victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Wirtz scored his fifth career Bundesliga goal in a 52 win against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a> on 6 February, becoming the first player in league history to reach this benchmark before turning eighteen years old.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> He extended his contract until 2026 on 3 May 2021, the day of his 18th birthday.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 28 November 2021, Wirtz netted his fifth Bundesliga goal of the season in a 13 win against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a> to become the first player under the age of 19 to score more than ten Bundesliga goals.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 15 December, he became the youngest player to reach 50 Bundesliga appearances against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">Hoffenheim</a>, at the age of 18 years and 223 days.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 March 2022, Wirtz tore his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anterior_cruciate_ligament" title="Anterior cruciate ligament">anterior cruciate ligament</a> in a 10 defeat against 1. FC Kln, hence he missed the rest of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2021%E2%80%9322_Bundesliga" title="202122 Bundesliga">202122 Bundesliga</a> season.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 22 January 2023, he played his first competitive match in ten months, coming off the bench, in a 32 away win over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mnchengladbach">Borussia Mnchengladbach</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-18"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="202324:_Domestic_double_and_player_of_the_season_award"><span id="2023.E2.80.9324:_Domestic_double_and_player_of_the_season_award"></span>202324: Domestic double and player of the season award</h4></div>
<p>On 26 October 2023, he scored a goal and provided a hat-trick of assists in a 51 victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Qaraba%C4%9F_FK" title="Qaraba FK">Qaraba</a> during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2023%E2%80%9324_UEFA_Europa_League" title="202324 UEFA Europa League">202324 Europa League</a> group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 14 April 2024, Wirtz scored his first career hat-trick, leading his team to a historic 50 title-clinching win over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a>, which gave Bayer their first <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deutsche_Meister" class="mw-redirect" title="Deutsche Meister">German championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-20"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> By the end of the season he would win the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024_DFB-Pokal_final" title="2024 DFB-Pokal final">DFB-Pokal final</a> in a 10 victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1._FC_Kaiserslautern" title="1. FC Kaiserslautern">Kaiserslautern</a> as well as reaching the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024_UEFA_Europa_League_final" title="2024 UEFA Europa League final">final</a> of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2023%E2%80%9324_UEFA_Europa_League" title="202324 UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a>. With twenty-two goal involvements throughout the season for his club in Bundesliga, he was voted player of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="202425:_DFL-Supercup_title_and_Champions_League_debut"><span id="2024.E2.80.9325:_DFL-Supercup_title_and_Champions_League_debut"></span>202425: DFL-Supercup title and Champions League debut</h4></div>
<p>In the beginning of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_Bundesliga" title="202425 Bundesliga">202425 season</a>, he would win the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024_DFL-Supercup" title="2024 DFL-Supercup">DFL-Supercup</a> with his team against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a> on penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-22"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>22<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> He made his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_UEFA_Champions_League" title="202425 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League debut</a> on the first matchday in a 40 away victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Feyenoord" title="Feyenoord">Feyenoord Rotterdam</a>, in which he scored a first-half brace and was named <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Player_of_the_match" title="Player of the match">Man of the Match</a>. On matchday two of the competition he would clinch the Man of the Match award for a second time in a 10 victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/AC_Milan" title="AC Milan">AC Milan</a>. He would go on to be determined Man of the Match two further times on matchday three in which he scored a goal in a 11 draw over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stade_Brestois_29" title="Stade Brestois 29">Brest</a> as well as matchday five in which he scored another first-half brace as well as giving an assist in the second half to help his team win 50 over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FC_Red_Bull_Salzburg" title="FC Red Bull Salzburg">Salzburg</a>. With five goals in five Champions League matches he became the first German to ever do that.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-23"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> His side would eventually be knocked out in the round of 16 by fellow Bundesliga side Bayern Munich 50 on aggregate, of which he missed the second leg match due to injury.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-24"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> 
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="International_career">International career</h2></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="2021:_Debut">2021: Debut</h3></div>
<p>Wirtz received his first call up to the senior team for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2022 FIFA World Cup">2022 FIFA World Cup</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2022 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">qualifiers</a> in March 2021 under <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Lw">Joachim Lw</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-25"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> He debuted on 2 September in a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_J" title="2022 FIFA World Cup qualification  UEFA Group J">World Cup qualifier</a> against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Liechtenstein_national_football_team" title="Liechtenstein national football team">Liechtenstein</a>, coming on as a substitute for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joshua_Kimmich" title="Joshua Kimmich">Joshua Kimmich</a> in the 82nd minute, ending in a 20 away victory for the Germans.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="2022:_World_Cup_and_injury">2022: World Cup and injury</h3></div>
<p>In May 2022, coach <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hansi_Flick" title="Hansi Flick">Hansi Flick</a> expressed his willingness to name Wirtz in the final squad for the 2022 FIFA World Cup, yet he missed the tournament due to his ACL injury.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-27"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="2024:_First_goals_and_Euros">2024: First goals and Euros</h3></div>
<p>On 23 March 2024, he scored his first ever goal for Germany in only seven seconds in a friendly match against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>, a 20 away victory, becoming the second fastest goalscorer in international football history behind <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austrian</a> footballer <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christoph_Baumgartner" title="Christoph Baumgartner">Christoph Baumgartner</a>, who scored a goal in just six seconds in another friendly match against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovakia_national_football_team" title="Slovakia national football team">Slovakia</a> on the same day.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-28"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-29"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 June 2024, Wirtz was named in Germany's squad for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2024" title="UEFA Euro 2024">UEFA Euro 2024</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On 14 June, he netted the opener of the tournament in a 51 victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland_national_football_team" title="Scotland national football team">Scotland</a>, becoming the youngest German player to score in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_Championship" title="European Championship">European Championship</a>, aged 21 years and 42 days, breaking the previous record of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kai_Havertz" title="Kai Havertz">Kai Havertz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> In the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2024_knockout_stage#Quarter-finals" title="UEFA Euro 2024 knockout stage">quarter-final</a> against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>, Wirtz replaced <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leroy_San%C3%A9" title="Leroy San">Leroy San</a> at half-time and scored an 89th-minute equalising goal which took the match to extra time. Spain went on to win 21 with a 119th-minute goal, knocking Germany out of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="202425:_UEFA_Nations_League"><span id="2024.E2.80.9325:_UEFA_Nations_League"></span>202425: UEFA Nations League</h3></div>
<p>In September 2024, Florian Wirtz made his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_UEFA_Nations_League" title="202425 UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League debut</a> in a 50 victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungary</a> with a goal and an assist. On matchday five of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">competition</a>, Wirtz would net his first ever <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_kick_(association_football)" title="Free kick (association football)">free-kick</a> of his professional career and score his first ever brace for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">German national team</a> in a 70 victory over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina_national_football_team" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina national football team">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a>. He would eventually top the group stage with his country and qualify for the quarter-finals against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, which he missed due to injury, but which Germany went on to win.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Style_of_play">Style of play</h2></div>
<p>Wirtz is an attacking midfielder, although he can also play wide as an inverted <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winger_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Winger (football)">winger</a>. He has a marked offensive mindset and is a very dynamic midfielder, who covers a lot of ground.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-33"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> He also was sometimes used as a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> or a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/False_nine" class="mw-redirect" title="False nine">false nine</a> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xabi_Alonso" title="Xabi Alonso">Xabi Alonso</a>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Personal_life">Personal life</h2></div>
<p>Wirtz's parents are his agents; his father, Hans-Joachim, is also chairman of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gr%C3%BCn-Wei%C3%9F_Brauweiler" class="mw-redirect" title="Grn-Wei Brauweiler">Grn-Wei Brauweiler</a>, the club that Wirtz played for as a child before joining <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1._FC_K%C3%B6ln" title="1. FC Kln">Kln</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-34"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> His elder sister <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Juliane_Wirtz" title="Juliane Wirtz">Juliane Wirtz</a> is a professional footballer as well.<sup id="cite_ref-Wonderkid_4-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florian_Wirtz#cite_note-Wonderkid-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</h2></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Club">Club</h3></div>
